class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/steam-typeface\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_steam_typeface.jpg\" width=\"1600\" height=\"1600\" alt=\"Steam Typeface\" title=\"Steam Typeface\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>09.24.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.tkqlhce.com/click-100493264-13915291?url=https://www.myfonts.com/fonts/spacetype/steam\">Steam</a> combines the spirit of the old-fashioned wood type with modern flavors. Its distinctive reversed high contrast and extremely bold serifs make it impossible to stay unnoticed.</p>\n\n<p>It’s a fun and bold unconventional typeface that we’ve designed with great passion and curiosity! The type family consists of 13 weights that are divided into several packs. Each font in the pack can be layered on top of each other to make a funkier look.</p>\n\n<p>Steam is multilingual! It speaks more than 130 languages and supports extended Latin, Cyrillic, punctuation, default and small numbers, symbols and signs. It is also familiar with the OpenType features like standard and discretionary ligatures, stylistic sets, localized forms, small numbers and fractions and more. </p>\n\n<p>Steam looks best on logos, posters, headlines, T-shirts and is perfect anytime you need some bold letters with specific flavor and touch.</p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/Jackcrossing\">Jack Crossing</a> is a graphic designer and image maker from London. He has an incredible portfolio, especially if you are into the 80s aesthetics of vintage chrome and neo-surrealistic subjects (if that’s even a term). One thing for sure, if you are like me, browsing through his work will bring you so many memories from the old days where the dream of a digital life was much nicer than what it turns out to be. Well, that was a bit too dramatic, but it sounded good, not as good as Jack’s.</p>\n\n<p>For more information make sure to check out <a            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/amazon-original-opener-3d-and-motion-design-case-study\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_amazon_original.jpg\" width=\"1600\" height=\"1600\" alt=\"Amazon Original Opener - 3D and Motion Design Case Study\" title=\"Amazon Original Opener - 3D and Motion Design Case Study\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>09.22.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/ethemcem\">Ethem Cem</a> shared a really awesome case study on 3D and motion where he had the opportunity to work with Creative Director Duncan Elms and Elastic to pitch frames for the Amazon Original's new opener.</p>\n\n<p>The first approach was to create a sequence in which the camera moves over changing landscapes. hills, tunnels, curved walls. The landscape is made up of light streaks. It begins with just light dots on the surface, then as light increases and grows in intensity it becomes light streaks. We travel over it and find the logo. </p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img alt=\"Image may contain: fireworks, light and screenshot\" src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/WZHbLOQcYJIvMk1W-5E2sVx9y9Z7dDDQPpo6A-aUnUA20XU6fQgNeRzN8BT8GNH-sIjdC0-jfERKc0w9EwETeEDDkgovWO2Bu-KZ9WeOLcdU_AX0bcdvbnEI2rm7-L30AcKFbFNG=s0\" /><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/qD5OO-2j52ohLLhhZGYgjjAZQkp6U2fSBSSTBlFaPoY9QOZAMu1dgnMEw7KsYrlL53OE3BMTjB9ovjYcriWsKC9rrF71QIwUy1SpS9EzLJXXIGRQ6PzaOaLgsPhSfGEWH5BkvEUY=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: light\" src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/CjJtcnHjV-1vMxukMI5dN8RsEBJOij3D5ktwSEABmn4CpV2P800tc00sUqsbCZYzwfG9wPQHS4LwPgpF4IMpRHGkQOzf8Q6G4fj82dHXpoCyGJ_yN5EK2mLT94xp5IEPkLMGlNvl=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: light\" src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/iZwg_DQxfV31I25SdaV__1dCNmoMpnsuc5r8aFULKHf2XAoi3RxUMnRGHFVVd6lCtQ8BciOjzlJxT9TyUEV9-kA2vOp6Eib-O1gWHXxtu-fk_IJn8gGgiptU653Y8jkomnDxAyxu=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: light and abstract\" src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/2YrdkeDPGicTvIX-KQzxyINy0ibYpK6Wc7ho7GJKlvSoOMSdhjhUSJo2MytYItvnSX9KfVL0wRf0n-fN94zYPPA23Mjz4yXRPFbdW5nAhRoqBIw4hAbgckT4RzGYXsfx-QJTBi8Y=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: light and fireworks\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/8Xno4cOIKt924bC-O3-gtxJc7uJ78t0Kp7up0tVoa6TxwzG3V3-TkoEh5tSsWkUmLBLUBs0Djo7hRBDmuGWuDw9rpvGOE9-kogzygHzulwgVbSEAQyuLd7suYxwMvYIMckzIdNmO=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: fireworks, light and stationary\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/EAX3-m9m6br8w8YEoHcOXMpBOh4VEnFDrMM0DY5FlHTKS1_42Zc--GgtAIIggQxZsT74lPp_nNdTthDJN8DQFgVhldRGCVq7XzuccGG5jfIFdGANYMT2ut8HveZRkw65WSGEKjBb=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: screenshot and abstract\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-X3CNfuy_EZ-_zqtpdSqG7YGZylt-8MmsK_q0iYUklyZ45RgQlaqXuFChvWdOYWaBhHcYJTAXZc_fgGtIhVexhZc9Sr6u9UANbiTeyvyyPDXATJM7mnAJFsYkN4PUeHlEvUPByHo=s0\" /></div>\n\n<p>The second approach is to create and feel abstract gradients. Seeing the light traveling over the close crops of the letters making different patterns over different shots. In some shots,  we tried to get the feeling that a light source is shining into the object to create the effect. The camera begins to pull out and we see the parts of letters with a prism effect. The camera keeps pulling out from a different angle, we see a light source shinned into it and realize this has a bit of a film projector feel.</p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img alt=\"Image may contain: abstract, electric blue and colorfulness\" src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/rDpsUThdZU8p_YP4LrpWphghqzwTdGr0ScYKCh7Nwi9Prl-FN5gIrSuXu3_kYRtL8pVfoymw_Dao5mvLXgw4xQmwRF_6x4Df2n75I1fNY6qGWW8RI-vfVq1rpB2snmQUDU3g88os=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: screenshot, indoor and abstract\" src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/Mlp5HnW31mzjgpds9qP3Kg7dYDuB3TW-DvFthf9Qy3DWgmxE9eQDTN-d_aqf2NbF1OsIVogJEQlAkhc4KWIPTAdSSD_dQMBSdOUkFB0mOYuogbYP8wjyeJ-_6sMCayWVaN5JoJZy=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: screenshot\" src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/htN3qzem5HWiBPkf7hmtGFuR2U7eY47XOSTSLPJxnk0a_6dfVLqbhfbHE8XJsD4cp55NwJMeL2RXoxj6BYDSitWu_DXvL0xzD1htJybfXfEhcbba8dwHwOg6SHayl1KCgvtISvKD=s0\" /><img src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/JH1R4m_zKBhA1zlpgcz6ESzcfhbQMZpt2KM6tWa5QTujKDnyN9F6GCbccuIrzntkMK4gTiJjS0-e26CJM442ip7ptwvpQq9jaXPyK3Uuig8vLtwhrFPywhSnPZAopW1E7BC_G_xL=s0\" /></div>\n\n<p>For the third approach, the idea was to create a place where everything should feel like a warm place we want to visit or be in. We tried to create a sequence that includes all stages of daylight. It starts with sunrise and we see close-ups from within letters looking around the environment. The camera pulls off and we see a wide letter in the environment at magic hour with two people in it. Then we see the letters are flying up into position in sunset lighting. And final lock-up on a blue gradient, lighter feeling in the late evening.</p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img alt=\"Image may contain: outdoor, cloud and sky\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/9fMY5mECVKMnPYPQhClUVUdRWzhuqV3_I3DWUil8Sc9q8wc390OOdAc8imaUEjkcJ3NeNq-vZZBAsaLppU1QrYP-IzIWIeZHgj0W4w7XN4ueyXUZhVZvO6TUArIv29LalrdYeiZV=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: cloud and sky\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/IHe7phWzmxqXKO9B7SNZffO4YbVPx6RFFlRvNnLwddZ_KOESgy6ZMj0HB9EUIX9xXHySSrbYxls8T8C4pjEgJFaa2Rr0x72dncQ7hm7yGUiKer0xceX_3X4xr9-kx-VC85FsBK5K=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: outdoor and sky\" src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/w_AbYpE893xtSLRAr-w6VpHgfocuoOG1CRdLu7Ph3lye__eyZM5Lt9RsJMhRiRRXVkqUNSm7KdXc6sKbIPsunknshraKq-FqeMz9tHG5D0fit_F0RbKHCc8dawv210xKeFFAN9WD=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: sky, beach and outdoor\" src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/1rHUpwarPkMakER_39HgFyL-VJzssuyUqe37xeJcOKzfQCTLMpD-60tDxl-MexQLIgYgEJjlyfJr-L7MONQGcAq1O6oZC4YKQDyr_WZlRW2A5gu2Q9yhsCE4MWQ9Sv2tPjL94cQJ=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: sky, cloud and outdoor\" src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/A9qQjaJ5Ke5MhyBUCBhUughXqAw6RHOcL-iURLht5xLmenU8z96zZwI5d3L6IFV3cedJ2T9yHS4IculuGcTt9qK_HIVziwezW-eFUf0I8rNbqt1Wk090vcAgZPvcfIW3r0q5yh9X=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: outdoor and screenshot\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/PsyWypO2lxCw7-cK9torBitVBSVrSYg5Q-6Hs6PWbKmZO1s_ombWJdpLccexapPrMxnxJmn1EtHPkIxAQIEDpMGyjJyqqcdcIqS6XG4PyOM0iytRmTJYuGB5n5T2y1S_PUutMbCA=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: screenshot, abstract and geometry\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/N9zP_JZgMJpRjDryey1uJ1LzomVvMD4XTy6yFDkfLb6pbsOvZ-qg1DV6BnA8h0Je7RUmGMCPyubP01S_9QJalATnr7Pn11kxbWlsqsuA3XC91D3gDp0SShOfMIjGSOqkgVjaWZ3M=s0\" /></div>\n\n<p>For the fourth approach, they tried to project different kinds of lights through the letters. Laser, projector, and more organic daylight. The idea was to set up huge interiors and use them as inside of the letters. They had projected the light to different kinds of surfaces like concrete, metallic, and glass. </p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>Our main goal was to emphasize the diversity of contents in Amazon by using different kinds of light sources.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/IsRhDOgwMu00eerGJTPcVu7Ccvf0PynkdFrzoH0cIFW8RftRwE_bprZg_7vIlNW6u1Lq4lsXAreg9twx1mznnJ6951TEfR7AP2wbQtHraPMaqUMPbVjmLTH5b9VoSxpUKyD6KaRm=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: sky and fog\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/61qN_0UN-YpaeyQMg8TyUgqzHYQxd25rEOZQqi4FNMQaioNR0h8ZdeGwjn7Ft82iARG5trFTP8g03YrrEPaUbbo8gYoFHE183KimCA090E-u7Ds7K3bGewpaaX_HRhXxTdq1yKnJ=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: abstract\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/7D4qONS9uFcFaP7XSLr4bwgp5gh4c7liYr_moYORsyqvCxvmP7RtdEWOPQmAQtaVsJ7UgS6VoJwKgfgMTU5B-lrwToinknzfx4qPDohNoT2cYb5RdNk6Q1s6Y0-9agLSzyCOgQBc=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: screenshot, abstract and monitor\" src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/hsJTGTPymk35DTURLyfsfiaUJSn_CSYMt0sfuDatD-qDcDbueuNai-SwZEu7Av_4eMClExn9C7tkd9M_cKIIr_sKnIg6JSdDDYio_Cm6K9jOAWPtotdJijXY-PsgfEMLE1Fy0Pnv=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: screenshot and art\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/abdBCx38dLAX8U7xgVKfF15FkJvpVGTkS916ByQF5BegbvCjWmOFiq32WfNEUBwy4i-dJ4QuyWESvmkLhETSIa5wVi6EIkntEv-IwCmNCvq7XctEAf5fnJLu5ETRtCqrOoveBxnR=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: screenshot\" src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/zYrT6PN8n1yHgFWBoAIY6JgfjwWaCZJ7IIeRJOYcDhycRa7kL5rnMOZ6X7rToLtDElxtnvJvgQHvAWqjLZ8LozJe6cD-2gl7TIh2zyCuNFt_Ab1IYHktChQqDPcgasjmV0opTI-q=s0\" /><img alt=\"Image may contain: abstract, indoor and geometry\" src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/wtCs77axEdC3_dWxwryifDehL-WgrHucYt2I4B3AUYOnuTJpvUlb3TEyD6zvN_BhywMnrx_Jlps8ZOwBJMtX74cCb0buUjqv0K6BqTuMhnDW1mKGep63HGfoAFnJ_pqLchQPZFGj=s0\" /></div>\n\n<p>The idea behind the fifth approach was to hide letters into architectural structures. Ethem and team tried to create hints in these structures by using the daylight and shadows. The sequence starts with geometric details from structures and slowly reveals the typography. </p>\n\n<p><q class=\"pullquote\">Our main inspiration for this concept was James Turrel's installations</q></p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img alt=\"Image may contain: wall, indoor and art\" class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/MariaGroenlund/\">Maria Grønlund</a> has shared an elegant series titled: <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/gallery/78688569/Waves-of-Light\">Waves of Light</a>. This is a return to her insanely popular and game-changing project '<a href=\"https://www.behance.net/gallery/9795093/I-speak-fluid-colors\">I speak fluid colors</a>' she published back in 2013. Still in the atmosphere of a study in colors and Illustrator techniques based on Illustrator blends tweaked in Photoshop. The results are just as mesmerizing as she originally worked which is pretty upscaling. Let's give it a look!</p>\n\n<blockquote>Colors communicate at the speed of light, speaking to all no matter what country or language is yours. Light waves travel from the sun through space and reach our eye in an instant. Wordlessly, poetic. 3D & Motion designer from Mexico City, Mexico. Working in collaboration with 'Character SF + NY', Rob was responsible for the 3D illustrations and animations. Under the direction of making 'real data', I love the 3D visual direction taken on how representative can data look if it was part of brand identity and I enjoyed the close-ups direction too. It's clever, simple, and shares a powerful identity. class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>09.25.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p dir=\"ltr\">It’s time for some digital art inspiration, today brought to you by the amazing people over at <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/olschinsky\">atelier olschinsky</a>. They create several concepts exploring a futuristic look really taking advantage of perspectives to create very stylish compositions. In addition to that we can see a masterful color selection, especially the second image from top to bottom. </p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\">Atelier Olschinsky, founded in 2002 is a small creative studio based in Vienna, Austria. Peter Olschinsky and Verena Weiss are operating in various fields such as graphic design, illustration, photography and art direction. In addition to their jobs for clients they also run several independent projects, always trying to develop and refine their work. </p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><q class=\"pullquote\">\"It is just so important to work as much as you can, to learn and to be open to new things. The journey is the award.\"</q></p>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\">Futuristic Digital Art</h2>\n\n<div class=\"imgsGrid\" dir=\"ltr\"><img property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>09.24.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/sameucliff/\">Samiran Borgohain</a> shared a 3D and motion design project / case study for JIPAAL. This project is about making the Artwork/Thumbnail of a song called 'JIPAAL' by Sannidhya Bhuyan, Tonmoy Krypton featuring Abhi Saikia. The word 'JIPAAL' is an Assamese word which means 'Freshness', specially the freshness brought by nature after a pleasant rainfall. This song is of Tropical Chill/ R&B genre and was released by <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/rainforestunderground/\">'Rainforest Underground'</a>, which is the sister record label of <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/rainforestrecords/\">'Rainforest Records'</a>.</p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img alt=\"art direction  artwork fresh motion graphics  music Nature Octane Render class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/beautiful-brand-identity-jays-coffee-brewers\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/fa481869918579.5b9179835f799.jpg\" width=\"2800\" height=\"1867\" alt=\"Beautiful Brand Identity for Jays Coffee Brewers\" title=\"Beautiful Brand Identity for Jays Coffee Brewers\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>09.25.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/dariastetsenko\">Daria Stetsenko</a> shared an awesome brand identity project on her Behance profile. It's titled Jays : Coffee Brewers and it is for a coffee shop in Zaporizhia, Ukraine. Main brand qualities are the local roast, arabica only menu, manual brewing, convenient location, and fast service. The brand philosophy is a faith in the great power of coffee that unites great people and creates a special moment of coziness by making our world a better place, one cup at a time. The target audience of the brand is active young people with positive thinking. </p>\n\n<p>The company was founded in 2012, and its old brand identity had the image of a flying bird that symbolizes freedom. Our task was to design a new logo and visual identity system. The primary requirements were the presence of a bird in the logo and black and white palette in combination with the brown color of kraft paper.  </p>\n\n<h2>Brand Identity</h2>\n\n<p><img src=\"https://mir-s3-cdn-cf.behance.net/project_modules/1400/3a0ef469918579.5b96302bb789f.jpg\" /></p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>We created a bird that symbolizes strength and lightness at the same time. Straightened wings tell us about freedom, goodwill, and openness. The typography system consists of a modern monospaced font that creates modest and straightforward brand character. The color palette allows the brand unobtrusively fit into the urban space. In addition to the visual identity system, we designed packaging, coffee cups, menu, business card, posters, stickers, and bag. The logo is manually printed on the packaging using a stamp to emphasize the individual brand approach to details. The label design is built on simple typography without decoration, focusing on the meaning, not the form.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<div class=\"imgsGrid\"><img
